<div id="review_2102064990" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2102064990" />
    <a title="Fiona" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/70584374-fiona"><img alt="Fiona" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1523885587p2/70584374.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2102064990?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Fiona" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Fiona" href="/user/show/70584374-fiona">Fiona</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2102064990" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6537098657262861648">The Rules of Survival was an amazing book. It is a story about three kids living with an abusive mother, the book takes you through their life, their struggles and adventures. The book has a very sad and sensitive subject, but the writing was so well done, it almost made me forget all the horrible situations that happened in this book. Many other good reads reviewers agree with this, some refer to this book as “haunting but beautiful” which is very poetic. I would agree with them, because there </span>
  <span id="freeText6537098657262861648" style="display:none">The Rules of Survival was an amazing book. It is a story about three kids living with an abusive mother, the book takes you through their life, their struggles and adventures. The book has a very sad and sensitive subject, but the writing was so well done, it almost made me forget all the horrible situations that happened in this book. Many other good reads reviewers agree with this, some refer to this book as “haunting but beautiful” which is very poetic. I would agree with them, because there were some times in the story were I needed to stop reading and process what horrible thing just happened, because I just put it aside in my head and focused on the writing style of the book. There were other times where I never wanted to stop reading and I couldn’t because Nancy Werlin is an amazing writer. I believe the writing is what made this book so amazing. <br /><br />For what Mathew has gone through I was constantly surprised he was remotely positive through the book; he had great advice to give to his little sister. Mathew said that “we should make fear our friend, instead of running away from it. Fear should be warning us when we are in danger, when we should save ourselves.” Mathew is very wise beyond his years, that’s why I liked his character so much. The character Murdoch was a very important character to the kids, but personally Murdoch did not make much of an impression on me; I think his character was just over rated and he got to much credit in the book. I definitely think he helped those kids tremendously, and had more courage than anyone,but overall I didn’t really like his personality.<br /><br />The book had some strengths and weaknesses. For example some parts were very boring and I could not encourage myself to read. The middle of the book is when it got kind of dull and not as interesting, however there were so many breathtaking moments of the book. The end for example, I never wanted to stop reading. The author did a good job on character development, you could really picture the characters physical appearance based off their descriptions and could sense their emotions by the writing styles Werlin used. I would recommend this book to other people who want to read a sad story, but with a happy ending. After reading The Rules of Survival I definitely want to read more of Nancy Werlin’s books. </span>
  <a data-text-id="6537098657262861648" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ng3aiGImKMn51aXa+o8P48+6WLwz64/mrXCtz2RNlcG7SY9pG8s39P4wDJ4PcYlG+CoU5rIFBh0M0nSTFswLsA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('WhbjvUwG6RaOh51dQft16dFXUcOfSGv+vcBumyiYqLl/UrZcNev2K4liNBm0BfNM5scdmR6m4gUcYrfHWhk2yA==')})
  }
